.addthis_floating_style {padding:0;border-radius:0;-webkit-border-radius:0;}
.addthis_32x32_style {width:32px;padding:4px;}
.addthis_floating_style .at300b, .addthis_floating_style .at300bo, .addthis_floating_style .at300m {padding:0;margin:0;}
.addthis_floating_style .at300b > *, .addthis_floating_style .at300bo > *, .addthis_floating_style .at300m > *, .addthis_floating_style.addthis_32x32_style a {margin-bottom:0;}
.addthis_floating_style.addthis_32x32_style, .addthis_floating_style.addthis_32x32_style .addthis_internal_container {width:32px;}
</style>
<script type="text/javascript">
var addthisHtml = '<div id="addthis_widget" class="addthis_toolbox addthis_floating_style addthis_32x32_style" style="height:128px;">';
addthisHtml += '<a class="addthis_button_facebook" style="cursor:pointer"></a>';
addthisHtml += '<a class="addthis_button_twitter" style="cursor:pointer"></a>';
addthisHtml += '<a class="addthis_button_google_plusone_share" style="cursor:pointer"></a>';
addthisHtml += '<a class="addthis_button_compact"  style="cursor:pointer"></a>';
addthisHtml += '</div>';

var offset = $('#panel-main').offset();
$('body').prepend(addthisHtml);
$('#addthis_widget').css({ position:'fixed', top:390, left:(offset.left - 36)});

$(window).resize(function () {
var offset = $('#panel-main').offset();
    $('#addthis_widget').css({ left:(offset.left - 36)});
});

$(window).scroll(function () {
    
    var addthisMaxScroll = offset.top + $('#panel-main').height() + 600 - $(window).height();
    if ($(window).scrollTop() > addthisMaxScroll) {
        if ($('#addthis_widget').css('display') != "none") {
            $('#addthis_widget').fadeOut(400, function () {});
        }
    }
    else {
        if ($('#addthis_widget').css('display') == "none") {
            $('#addthis_widget').fadeIn(400, function () {});
        }
    }
});
</script>
